Plus, if someone accidentally drops one, it's completely covered so it can still be safely used! Made of all white birch, these toothpicks are incredibly solid, smooth, and burr free, and they are less likely to splinter during use. With no added flavor or color, these plain toothpicks are sure to meet the needs of every customer. Packaged in a convenient self-dispensing box, these toothpicks can be placed out for grabs next to your hostess stand, at your concierge counter or dining room tables.

	simple	pack-3-0240	Hotpack - Children's Face Mask 3 Ply Non-Woven With Ear Loop (5 Designs In One Box) - 50 pcs	KFMD			50 pcs	1	0	visible	Hotpack - Children's Face Mask 3 Ply Non-Woven With Ear Loop (5 Designs In One Box) - 50 pcs	"Hotpack - Children's Face Mask 3 Ply Non-Woven With Ear Loop (5 Designs In One Box) - 50 pcs - Children should read and correctly understand the instructions before wearing them with the help of their parent’s in-
1: Parents should always pay attention to the wearing of children's masks, if children feel unwell while wearing masks should promptly adjust or stop using.
2: Children are not advised to wear adult masks with a tightness requirement because of the small size of the child's face and the inability to fitfully with the edges of the adult mask.
3: Children with respiratory distress, vomiting, irritability, and sleepiness are not suitable for wearing masks.
